function create_ezolpl() {
    var d = new Date();
    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (365*24*60*60*1000));
    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
    document.cookie = "ezux_lpl_1700=" + new Date().getTime() + "|47710ae0-bdb2-48da-6345-fc81cb2cb225; " + expires;
}
function attach_ezolpl() {
    if(window.attachEvent) {
        window.attachEvent('onload', create_ezolpl);
    } else {
        if(window.onload) {
            var curronload = window.onload;
            var newonload = function(evt) {
                curronload(evt);
                create_ezolpl();
            };
            window.onload = newonload;
        } else {
            window.onload = create_ezolpl;

  <script data-cfasync="false" data-pagespeed-no-defer type="text/javascript">
function ez_isclean( data ) {
    if (typeof data === 'undefined') { data = document.URL; }
    var re = /(([^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+(\.[^<>()[\]\\.,;:\s@\"]+)*)|(\".+\"))(@|%2540|%40)((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))/;
    var isClean = !re.test(data);
    return isClean;
}

var ez_queue = new Array();
function sort_queue(a, b)
{
  if( a.priority < b.priority ) return -1;
  else if( a.priority == b.priority ) return 0;
  else return 1;
}
function execute_ez_queue()
{
  ez_queue.sort( sort_queue );

  for( var i in ez_queue )
  {
        if(typeof ez_queue[i].method != "undefined")
        {
            try{
                ez_queue[i].method.call( null );
            }
            catch (err) {

            }
        }
  }
}

window.ez_ad_units = new Array();
window.ezslots = new Array();
function ez_write_tag(d) {
    if(ez_isclean() && d instanceof Array) {

		ez_ad_units[ez_ad_units.length] = d;
        var ezcmd = "googletag.cmd.push(function() {var divid = 'div-gpt-ad-"+d[1]+"-0';if(typeof ezlrarn == 'function'){ezlrarn(divid);}googletag.display(divid);var to = 0;if("+d[2]+".getTargeting('ga')[0] == '0'){to = 500;console.log('"+d[2]+" - no google');}if(window.ezDisableInitialLoad==true){setTimeout(function(){googletag.pubads().refresh(["+d[2]+"])},to);}});";
		return ezcmd;
    }
    else {
        return "1+1";
    }
}
function in_array(needle, haystack) {
    var length = haystack.length;
    for(var i = 0; i < length; i++) {
        if(haystack[i] == needle) return true;
    }
    return false;
}

                         <div class="excerpt-text" eza="cwidth:608px;;cheight:115px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:105px;wocalc:105px;hcalc:759px;rend_px_area:69920;" cwidth="608" style="background-color:transparent;color:rgb(70, 70, 70);font-family:Roboto, sans-serif;font-size:17px;font-weight:300;line-height:23px;nodepath:/html/body/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div[1]/div/article/div/div[1];pagepos:120;cwidth:608px;cheight:115px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:105px;hcalc:759;rend_px_area:69920;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:119;req_px_area:73416;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:23;req_margin_and_padding:23;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:0;parent-line-height:19px;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;"> 
                          <p eza="cwidth:608px;;cheight:115px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:105px;wocalc:105px;hcalc:736px;rend_px_area:69920;" cwidth="608" style="background-color:transparent;nodepath:/html/body/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div[1]/div/article/div/div[1]/p;pagepos:121;cwidth:608px;cheight:115px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:170px;wocalc:105px;hcalc:736;rend_px_area:69920;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:119;req_px_area:73416;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:23;req_margin_and_padding:23;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:23;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 23px 0px;margin:0px 0px 23px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">For my job I constantly have to convert from Euros to US Dollars, with some other currencies thrown in by overseas customers to keep things complicated. Ive been using an app on my iPhone for this but Im confident that theres a smarter solution for currency conversion on my computer. Whats your suggestion, Dave?</p> 
                         </div>
                         <p eza="cwidth:608px;;cheight:475px;;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:96px;wocalc:96px;hcalc:1786px;rend_px_area:288800;" cwidth="608" style="background-color:transparent;nodepath:/html/body/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div/div/div/div[3]/div/div/div[1]/div/article/div/p[1];pagepos:129;cwidth:608px;cheight:475px;wcalc_source:child;wcalc:96px;wocalc:96px;hcalc:1786;rend_px_area:288800;rcnt:1;ez_min_text_wdth:114;req_px_area:215232;obj_px_area:0;req_px_height:19;req_margin_and_padding:18;req_ns_height:;vertical_margin:18;parent-line-height:19px;margin-for-scale:0px 0px 18px 0px;margin:0px 0px 18px 0px;padding-for-scale:0px 0px 0px 0px;">As someone who was born overseas, I pay perhaps an atypical level of attention to the currency market, trying to track the relative worth of goods as things fluctuate. And fluctuate they do, the currency market is extraordinarily volatile and its awful easy to lose a lot of money on a transaction like an overseas hotel reservation if youre not paying close attention. And those Euros and Pounds, Yen and Lira that youve kept as souvenirs? Yeah, as the market fluctuates those can end up devaluing even as they just sit innocently in your scrapbook.<br> There are a ton of different ways to convert currencies too, and Id never even thought about using an Apple iPhone app. A quick search reveals over 150 applications in this space. What the deuce?! Is there that much variation in this fairly straightforward calculation??<br> Anyway, Ill highlight three ways you can quickly and easily convert from one currency to another, using as my example the calculation of the USD equivalent of 100 British Pounds Sterling.<br> The first way, the one I prefer, is to use Google. Yup, a quick Google search in the correct format and itll figure out the results right there in the search engine:<br> </p>
